<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:breken.html>breken</a></i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
